original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if(reset)
            q <= 4'd0;
        else begin
            q[3] <= q[2];
            q[2] <= q[1];
            q[1] <= q[0];
            q[0] <= ~q[3];
        end
    end

endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

                    q[3] <= q[2];

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @ (posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if(reset)
            q <= 4'd0;
        else begin
            q <= q + 4'd1;
            if(q == 4'd9)
                q <= 4'd0;
        end
    end

endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if(reset)
            q <= 4'd0;
        else begin
            q[3] <= q[2];
            q[2] <= q[1];
            q[1] <= q[0];
            q[0] <= 1'b0;
        end
    end

endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if(reset)
            q <= 4'd0;
        else begin
            q[3] <= q[2];
            q[2] <= q[1];
            q[1] <= q[0];
            q[0] <= 1'b1;
        end
    end

endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= 1'b1;
                end
        end
endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= 1'b1;
                end
        end

endmodule

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @ (posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

endmodule

module top_module (

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

    input clk,

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= 1'b0;
                end
        end

endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)

            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                q <= q + 4'd1;
        end
endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= 1'b0;
                end
        end

endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if(reset)
            q <= 4'd0;
        else begin
            q <= q + 4'd1;
        end
    end

endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)

            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= 1'b1;
                end
        end

endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @ (posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                q <= q + 4'd1;
        end
endmodule

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

            else

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if(reset)
            q <= 4'd0;
        else begin
            q[3] <= q[2];
            q[2] <= q[1];
            q[1] <= q[0];
            q[0] <= ~q[3];
        end
    end
endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= 1'b0;
                end
        end

endmodule

// Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if(reset)
            q <= 4'd0;
        else begin
            q <= q + 4'd1;
        end
    end
endmodule

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk)
        begin
            if(reset)
                q <= 4'd0;
            else
                begin
                    q[3] <= q[2];
                    q[2] <= q[1];
                    q[1] <= q[0];
                    q[0] <= ~q[3];
                end
        end

original text:  // Build a decade counter that counts from 0 through 9, inclusive, with a period of 10. The reset input is synchronous, and should reset the counter to 0.

module top_module (
    input clk,
    input reset,        // Synchronous active-high reset
    output [3:0] q);

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if(reset)
            q <= 4'd0;
        else begin
            q[3] <= q[2];
            q[2] <= q[1];
            q[1] <= q[0];
            q[0] <= 1'b1;
        end
    end

endmodule
